    window.awLoadAds = function( options ){
                        if ( typeof window.awAdsLoaded === 'undefined' ) {
                            window.awAdsLoaded = true;
                            options = options || {
                                /* Default options. */
                                usePersonalizedAds: true
                            };

                            var utmVars = [
                                'utm_source', 
                                'utm_medium', 
                                'utm_campaign', 
                                'utm_term', 
                                'utm_content'
                            ];

                            var utmVarsTargeting = []

                            utmVars.forEach( function( utmVarName ){
                                var utmVarValue = getParameterByName( utmVarName );
                                if ( utmVarValue ){
                                    utmVarsTargeting.push({
                                        utmVarName: utmVarName,
                                        utmVarValue: utmVarValue                             
                                    })
                                }
                            } );

                            

                            jQuery.getScript( 'https://cdn1.htlbid.com/v3/adweek.com/htlbid.js', function( data, textStatus, jqxhr ) {
                                if ( jqxhr.status === 200 ){
                                    var htlbid = window.htlbid || {};
                                    htlbid.cmd = htlbid.cmd || [];
                                    htlbid.cmd.push(function() {
                                        if ( options.usePersonalizedAds === true ){
                                            htlbid.setRequestNonPersonalizedAds( 0 );                                  
                                        } else {
                                            htlbid.setRequestNonPersonalizedAds( 1 );
                                        }

                                        htlbid.setTargeting( 'testing', 'no');htlbid.setTargeting( 'page', '1280126' );htlbid.setTargeting( 'term', ["Homepage"] );htlbid.setTargeting( 'zone', 'Homepage' ) 

                                        if ( utmVarsTargeting && utmVarsTargeting.length > 0 ){
                                            utmVarsTargeting.forEach( function( utmVar ){
                                                htlbid.setTargeting( utmVar.utmVarName, utmVar.utmVarValue );
                                            } );
                                        }
                                        
                                        if ( window.location.href.indexOf( 'presentation=on' ) > -1 ){
                                            htlbid.setTargeting( 'presentation', 'on' );
                                        }

                                        htlbid.on('occupied', function(slot) {
                                            var div = jQuery( '#' + slot.getId() );
                                            div.addClass( 'htl-ad-occupied' );


                                            if ( div.hasClass( 'htl-ad-occupied' ) ){
                                                if ( div.hasClass( 'aw-ad-unit-m1' ) && div.height() < 600 ){
                                                    div.css( { 'min-height': 'auto' } );
                                                }

                                                if ( div.hasClass( 'aw-ad-unit-t' ) && div.height() < 300 ){
                                                    div.css( { 'min-height': 'auto' } );
                                                }
                                            }
                                        });                                        

                                        htlbid.on('empty', function(slot) {
                                            var div = document.getElementById(slot.getId());
                                            try{
                                                var adWrapper = div.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode;
                                                if ( adWrapper.className.indexOf( 'mobile-ad' ) > -1 ){
                                                    adWrapper.classList.add( 'htl-ad-empty' );
                                                }
                                            } catch(err){ /* noop */ }
                                        });
                                    });
                                }  
                            });
                        }
                    }
   </script>

    function uuidProfileCall() {
			var rootUrl = 'https://api.parsely.com/v2/profile?apikey=adweek.com';
			var uuid = '&uuid=' + PARSELY.config.parsely_site_uuid;
			var requestUrl = rootUrl + uuid + '&url=' + window.location.href;
			jQuery.ajax({
				url: requestUrl,
				dataType: "jsonp"
			});
		}

		if (typeof PARSELY == 'object') {
			var oldonload = PARSELY.onload;
			if (typeof PARSELY.onload != 'function') {
				PARSELY.onload = uuidProfileCall
			}
			else {
				PARSELY.onload = function () {
					if (oldonload) {
						oldonload();
					}
					uuidProfileCall();
				};
			}
		}

		else {
			PARSELY = {
				onload: uuidProfileCall
			}
		}

                    'use strict';
                    // Determine whether to load personalized or non-personalized ads

                    if( typeof window.awLoadAds !== 'undefined' ){
                        if ( typeof otGeoContinent !== 'undefined' && otGeoContinent === 'EU' ) {
                            window.awLoadAds( {
                                usePersonalizedAds: OnetrustActiveGroups.includes( 'C0004' )
                            } );
                        } else {
                            window.awLoadAds( {
                                usePersonalizedAds: true
                            } );
                        }
                    }

                    var myIP,
                        ajaxurl = window.location.origin + '/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';

                    window.lytics = window.lytics || {};
                    window.lytics.fields = window.lytics.fields || {};

                    var userCountryCode = 'unknown';
                    var locationCookie = Cookies.get( 'locationCookie' );

                    var locationData = {
                        ip: 'unknown',
                        country: {
                            iso_code: 'unknown'
                        }
                    };

                    function awProcessUserLocation( locationData ){

                        if ( locationData && locationData.country && locationData.country.iso_code ) {
                            userCountryCode = locationData.country.iso_code;

                            $( document ).trigger( 'aw-location-detected', locationData );

                        }
                        window.lytics.fields.attr_user_country_code = userCountryCode;
                    }

                    if ( typeof locationCookie === 'undefined' ) {
                        // If location cookie does not exist
                        jQuery.ajax( {
                            type: 'GET',
                            url: 'https://api.ipify.org?format=json'
                        } ).done( function ( data ) {
                            var ipAddress = ( data && data.ip ) || false;
                            $( document ).trigger( 'aw-ip-detected', ipAddress );
                            $( 'head' ).append( '<meta name="ipaddr" value="' + ipAddress + '" />' );

                            if ( ipAddress ) {
                                myIP = data.ip;
                                locationData.ip = data.ip;
                                jQuery.post(
                                    ajaxurl,
                                    { action: 'get_user_location', userIP: myIP },
                                    function( response ) {
                                        var locationResponse = JSON.parse( response );

                                        // if response contains country and iso_code
                                        
                                        if ( locationResponse.country && locationResponse.country.iso_code ){
                                            locationData.country.iso_code = locationResponse.country.iso_code;
                                            var cookieLocStr = JSON.stringify( locationData );
                                            Cookies.set( 'locationCookie', cookieLocStr, { expires: 1 } );
                                        } else {
                                            // else if response does not contain country and iso_code
                                            // create cookie with default locationData
                                            var cookieLocStr = JSON.stringify( locationData );
                                            Cookies.set( 'locationCookie', cookieLocStr, { expires: 1 } );
                                        }
                                        awProcessUserLocation( locationData );
                                    }
                                );
                            }
                        } );
                    } else {
                        var parsedCookie = JSON.parse( locationCookie );
                        locationData.ip = parsedCookie.ip;
                        locationData.country.iso_code = parsedCookie.country.iso_code;
                        $( document ).trigger( 'aw-ip-detected', locationData.ip );
                        $( 'head' ).append( '<meta name="ipaddr" value="' + locationData.ip + '" />' );
                        awProcessUserLocation( locationData );
                    }
            })(jQuery);
   </script>
